In the ‘a’ in Om and in the word ‘N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa ’ occurring in aс╣гс╣н─Бkс╣гara,
the supreme end of life (i.e.) Bhagav─Бn,
who is opposed to all that is objectionable or faulty, is indicated;

in the ’m’ in ‘om’ and in the part ’n─Бra’ occurring in N─Бr─Бyaс╣З─Бya,
the essential nature (svar┼лpa) of the j─лva
who is to attain this end is disclosed;

the means of attainment already existing as established (siddha up─Бya) namely, Bhagav─Бn,
is indicated in the part “ayana” occurring in N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa
and the means to be accomplished or adopted (s─Бdhya up─Бya ), which is self-surrender, is in namas;
the fruit desired, viz., the enjoyment of Brahman which includes also service to Him+++(5)+++
is disclosed in the dative or fourth case in N─Бr─Бyaс╣З─Бya;
the hindrance to it, namely, the feeling of ‘mine’
is in the word mama occurring in namah (na mama ).
He who understands the Aс╣гс╣н─Бkс╣гara mantra
that reveals all these five
and 1 Dvayam too, which is to the same effect–
he will be considered by all as one who knows everything.

English

All these hindrances to mokс╣гa are to be understood
in whatever is contrary to what is ordained in the three mysteries (mantras)
(e. g. the feeling that the j─лva is independent
and acts for his own purposes
which is opposed to the truths shown in the aс╣гс╣н─Бkс╣гara),
in the egoism, or sense of ‘my’ or ‘mine’ in the genitive mama in namah (na + mama)
and also in the words тАШall thy sins’ in the carama ┼Ыloka .

These have to be thought of,
so that one may feel the suffering
which lies in walking on the hot sands of saс╣Бs─Бra
and desire to hasten towards the path leading to bliss.

Espa├▒ol

Todos estos obst├бculos para mokс╣гa
deben ser entendidos
en lo que sea contrario a lo que se ordena en los tres misterios (mantras)
(por ejemplo, la sensaci├│n de que el J─лva es independiente
y act├║a para sus propios fines
que se opone a las verdades
que se muestran en el aс╣гс╣н─Бkс╣гara),
en el ego├нsmo, o sentido de ‘mi’ o ‘m├нo’ en la mam├б genitiva en Namah (Na + Mama)
y tambi├йn en las palabras
“todos tus pecados” en el Carama ┼Ъloka.

Estos tienen que ser pensados en
para que uno pueda sentir el sufrimiento
que se encuentra en caminar sobre las arenas calientes de Saс╣Бs─Бra
y deseo de apresurarse hacia
el camino que conduce a la dicha.

English

Those who know these five have declared them
in order that I may not despair in mind
and in order that the darkness of ignorance may not confound me-
the five namely -

  • the Lord of the lotus-born Lakс╣гm─л , who stands as the one thing to be attained,
  • the j─лva who loves the lord and craves for His grace by seeking His feet,
  • the means (or up─Бya) to be adopted by the j─лva for the attainment,
  • and the fruit resulting therefrom,
  • as also the strong fetters of sin due to delusion or ignorance (which are hindrances).
Espa├▒ol

Aquellos que conocen estos cinco los han declarado
Para que no pueda desesperar en mente
y para que la oscuridad de la ignorancia no me confunda
los cinco a saber:

  • el se├▒or del Lakс╣гm─л nacida en el loto ,
    quien se destaca como la ├║nica cosa que se puede alcanzar,
  • El J─лva que ama al Se├▒or y anhela su gracia buscando sus pies,
  • Los medios (o up─Бya) ser├бn adoptados por el J─лva para el logro,
  • y la fruta que resulta de all├н,
  • como tambi├йn las fuertes grifos del pecado debido a la ilusi├│n o la ignorancia (que son obst├бculos).

English

That which is to be attained
is the Supreme Brahman who is the ┼Ыeс╣г─л of all;
I am also a fit person to attain Him;
the attainment should come to me as inheritance
due naturally to me as to the S┼лris;
alas, by my egoism and the ignorance arising from it, I have lost it,
but I have been taught that, by surrendering myself to the divine couple who are my ┼Ыeс╣г─лs,
I can now attain it.

Espa├▒ol

Tambi├йn soy una persona en forma para alcanzarlo;
El logro deber├нa llegar a m├н como herencia
Debido naturalmente a m├н en cuanto a los s┼лris;
por desgracia, por mi ego├нsmo y la ignorancia que surge de ├йl,
lo he perdido,
Pero me han ense├▒ado que,
al entregarme a la pareja divina, que son mis ┼Ъeс╣г─лs,
Ahora puedo alcanzarlo.

  79. The eight kinds of siddhi:
    Aс╣Зim─Б (contraction of one’s body to the size of an atom),
    mahima (assuming a huge form) Laghim─Б (making one’s body light)
    Garim─Б (making the body heavy),
    va┼Ыitvam (mastery over self),
    ai┼Ыvaryam (lordship)
    pr─Бpti (the power of obtaining whatever one wants)
    and pr─Бk─Бmyam (perfect freedom of the will.) ↩︎
